[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m [prompt] system
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m You are a helpful AI Assistant, designed to provide well-reasoned and detailed responses. You FIRST think about the reasoning process step by step and then provide the user with the answer. Please enclose your final answer in the box: \boxed{Your Answer}.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m user
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m Bin $A$ has one white ball and four black balls.  Bin $B$ has three balls labeled $\$1$ and one ball labeled $\$7$.  Bin $W$ has five balls labeled $\$8$ and one ball labeled $\$500$.  A game is played as follows: a ball is randomly selected from bin $A$.  If it is black, then a ball is randomly selected from bin $B$; otherwise, if the original ball is white, then a ball is randomly selected from bin $W$.  You win the amount printed on the second ball selected.  What is your expected win?
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m assistant
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m [response] To determine the expected win in this game, we need to consider the probabilities of each scenario and the corresponding winnings. Let's break it down step by step.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 1. **Probability of selecting a black ball from bin \( A \):**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    Bin \( A \) has 1 white ball and 4 black balls. Therefore, the probability of selecting a black ball from bin \( A \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    P(\text{Black from } A) = \frac{4}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 2. **Probability of selecting a white ball from bin \( A \):**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    The probability of selecting a white ball from bin \( A \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    P(\text{White from } A) = \frac{1}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 3. **Probability of selecting a ball from bin \( B \) given that a black ball is selected from bin \( A \):**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    Bin \( B \) has 3 balls labeled \$1 and 1 ball labeled \$7. Therefore, the probability of selecting a ball from bin \( B \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    P(\text{Ball from } B \mid \text{Black from } A) = \frac{3}{4}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 4. **Probability of selecting a ball from bin \( W \) given that a white ball is selected from bin \( A \):**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    Bin \( W \) has 5 balls labeled \$8 and 1 ball labeled \$500. Therefore, the probability of selecting a ball from bin \( W \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    P(\text{Ball from } W \mid \text{White from } A) = \frac{1}{6}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 5. **Expected win if a black ball is selected from bin \( A \):**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    If a black ball is selected from bin \( A \), the next ball selected is from bin \( B \). The expected value of the winnings in this case is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    E(\text{Win} \mid \text{Black from } A) = 1 \cdot \frac{3}{4} + 7 \cdot \frac{1}{4} = \frac{3}{4} + \frac{7}{4} = \frac{10}{4} = 2.5
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 6. **Expected win if a white ball is selected from bin \( A \):**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    If a white ball is selected from bin \( A \), the next ball selected is from bin \( W \). The expected value of the winnings in this case is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    E(\text{Win} \mid \text{White from } A) = 8 \cdot \frac{1}{6} + 500 \cdot \frac{5}{6} = \frac{8}{6} + \frac{2500}{6} = \frac{2508}{6} = 418
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 7. **Total expected win:**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    The total expected win is the weighted average of the expected wins from both scenarios, weighted by their respective probabilities:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    E(\text{Total Win}) = P(\text{Black from } A) \cdot E(\text{Win} \mid \text{Black from } A) + P(\text{White from } A) \cdot E(\text{Win} \mid \text{White from } A)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    Substituting the values we have:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    E(\text{Total Win}) = \frac{4}{5} \cdot 2.5 + \frac{1}{5} \cdot 418 = \frac{10}{5} + \frac{418}{5} = \frac{428}{5} = 85.6
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m Therefore, the expected win is \(\boxed{85.6}\).

[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m [prompt] system
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m You are a helpful AI Assistant, designed to provide well-reasoned and detailed responses. You FIRST think about the reasoning process step by step and then provide the user with the answer. Please enclose your final answer in the box: \boxed{Your Answer}.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m user
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m Bin $A$ has one white ball and four black balls.  Bin $B$ has three balls labeled $\$1$ and one ball labeled $\$7$.  Bin $W$ has five balls labeled $\$8$ and one ball labeled $\$500$.  A game is played as follows: a ball is randomly selected from bin $A$.  If it is black, then a ball is randomly selected from bin $B$; otherwise, if the original ball is white, then a ball is randomly selected from bin $W$.  You win the amount printed on the second ball selected.  What is your expected win?
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m assistant
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m [response] To determine the expected win in the game, we need to consider the probabilities of each scenario and the corresponding winnings. Let's break down the problem step by step.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 1. **Probability of selecting a black ball from bin \(A\):**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    Bin \(A\) has 1 white ball and 4 black balls. Therefore, the probability of selecting a black ball from bin \(A\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    P(\text{black from } A) = \frac{4}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    If a black ball is selected from bin \(A\), then a ball is randomly selected from bin \(B\). Bin \(B\) has 3 balls labeled \$1 and 1 ball labeled \$7. The probability of selecting a ball labeled \$1 from bin \(B\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    P(\$1 \text{ from } B \mid \text{black from } A) = \frac{3}{4}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    The probability of selecting a ball labeled \$7 from bin \(B\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    P(\$7 \text{ from } B \mid \text{black from } A) = \frac{1}{4}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    The expected value of the winnings if a black ball is selected from bin \(A\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    E(\text{winnings} \mid \text{black from } A) = \$1 \cdot \frac{3}{4} + \$7 \cdot \frac{1}{4} = \frac{3}{4} + \frac{7}{4} = \$5
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 2. **Probability of selecting a white ball from bin \(A\):**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    The probability of selecting a white ball from bin \(A\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    P(\text{white from } A) = \frac{1}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    If a white ball is selected from bin \(A\), then a ball is randomly selected from bin \(W\). Bin \(W\) has 5 balls labeled \$8 and 1 ball labeled \$500. The probability of selecting a ball labeled \$8 from bin \(W\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    P(\$8 \text{ from } W \mid \text{white from } A) = \frac{5}{6}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    The probability of selecting a ball labeled \$500 from bin \(W\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    P(\$500 \text{ from } W \mid \text{white from } A) = \frac{1}{6}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    The expected value of the winnings if a white ball is selected from bin \(A\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    E(\text{winnings} \mid \text{white from } A) = \$8 \cdot \frac{5}{6} + \$500 \cdot \frac{1}{6} = \frac{40}{6} + \frac{500}{6} = \frac{540}{6} = \$90
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 3. **Total expected value of the winnings:**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    The total expected value of the winnings is the weighted average of the expected values from the two scenarios, weighted by their probabilities:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    E(\text{winnings}) = P(\text{black from } A) \cdot E(\text{winnings} \mid \text{black from } A) + P(\text{white from } A) \cdot E(\text{winnings} \mid \text{white from } A)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    Substituting the values we found:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    E(\text{winnings}) = \frac{4}{5} \cdot 5 + \frac{1}{5} \cdot 90 = \frac{20}{5} + \frac{90}{5} = \frac{110}{5} = \$22
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m Therefore, the expected win is \(\boxed{22}\).

[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m You are a helpful AI Assistant, designed to provide well-reasoned and detailed responses. You FIRST think about the reasoning process step by step and then provide the user with the answer. Please enclose your final answer in the box: \boxed{Your Answer}.

[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m Bin $A$ has one white ball and four black balls.  Bin $B$ has three balls labeled $\$1$ and one ball labeled $\$7$.  Bin $W$ has five balls labeled $\$8$ and one ball labeled $\$500$.  A game is played as follows: a ball is randomly selected from bin $A$.  If it is black, then a ball is randomly selected from bin $B$; otherwise, if the original ball is white, then a ball is randomly selected from bin $W$.  You win the amount printed on the second ball selected.  What is your expected win?
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m assistant
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m [response] To determine the expected win in the game, we need to consider the probabilities of each scenario and the corresponding winnings. Let's break it down step by step.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 1. **Probability of selecting a black ball from bin \( A \):**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    Bin \( A \) has 1 white ball and 4 black balls. Therefore, the probability of selecting a black ball from bin \( A \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    P(\text{black from } A) = \frac{4}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    If a black ball is selected from bin \( A \), a ball is then selected from bin \( B \). Bin \( B \) has 3 balls labeled \$1 and 1 ball labeled \$7. Therefore, the probability of selecting a ball labeled \$1 from bin \( B \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    P(\$1 \mid \text{black from } A) = \frac{3}{4}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    The probability of selecting a ball labeled \$7 from bin \( B \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    P(\$7 \mid \text{black from } A) = \frac{1}{4}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    The expected value of the winnings if a black ball is selected from bin \( A \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    E(\$1 \mid \text{black from } A) \cdot P(\$1 \mid \text{black from } A) + E(\$7 \mid \text{black from } A) \cdot P(\$7 \mid \text{black from } A) = \$1 \cdot \frac{3}{4} + \$7 \cdot \frac{1}{4} = \frac{3}{4} + \frac{7}{4} = \$5
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 2. **Probability of selecting a white ball from bin \( A \):**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    The probability of selecting a white ball from bin \( A \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    P(\text{white from } A) = \frac{1}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    If a white ball is selected from bin \( A \), a ball is then selected from bin \( W \). Bin \( W \) has 5 balls labeled \$8 and 1 ball labeled \$500. Therefore, the probability of selecting a ball labeled \$8 from bin \( W \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    P(\$8 \mid \text{white from } A) = \frac{5}{6}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    The probability of selecting a ball labeled \$500 from bin \( W \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    P(\$500 \mid \text{white from } A) = \frac{1}{6}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    The expected value of the winnings if a white ball is selected from bin \( A \) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    E(\$8 \mid \text{white from } A) \cdot P(\$8 \mid \text{white from } A) + E(\$500 \mid \text{white from } A) \cdot P(\$500 \mid \text{white from } A) = \$8 \cdot \frac{5}{6} + \$500 \cdot \frac{1}{6} = \frac{40}{6} + \frac{500}{6} = \frac{540}{6} = \$90
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 3. **Total expected win:**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    The total expected win is the sum of the expected wins from both scenarios:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    E(\text{total win}) = P(\text{black from } A) \cdot E(\$1 \mid \text{black from } A) + P(\text{white from } A) \cdot E(\$8 \mid \text{white from } A) = \frac{4}{5} \cdot 5 + \frac{1}{5} \cdot 90 = 4 + 18 = \$22
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m Therefore, the expected win is \(\boxed{22}\).

[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m [prompt] system
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m You are a helpful AI Assistant, designed to provide well-reasoned and detailed responses. You FIRST think about the reasoning process step by step and then provide the user with the answer. Please enclose your final answer in the box: \boxed{Your Answer}.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m user
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m Bin $A$ has one white ball and four black balls.  Bin $B$ has three balls labeled $\$1$ and one ball labeled $\$7$.  Bin $W$ has five balls labeled $\$8$ and one ball labeled $\$500$.  A game is played as follows: a ball is randomly selected from bin $A$.  If it is black, then a ball is randomly selected from bin $B$; otherwise, if the original ball is white, then a ball is randomly selected from bin $W$.  You win the amount printed on the second ball selected.  What is your expected win?
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m assistant
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m [response] To determine the expected win in the game, we need to calculate the expected value of the amount won based on the probabilities of selecting each type of ball from bins \(A\) and \(W\), and then the probabilities of selecting each type of ball from bin \(B\).
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 1. **Calculate the probability of selecting a black ball from bin \(A\):**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    Bin \(A\) has 4 black balls and 1 white ball, so the total number of balls in bin \(A\) is \(4 + 1 = 5\).
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    The probability of selecting a black ball from bin \(A\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    P(\text{black from } A) = \frac{4}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 2. **Calculate the probability of selecting a white ball from bin \(A\):**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    The probability of selecting a white ball from bin \(A\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    P(\text{white from } A) = \frac{1}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 3. **Calculate the probability of selecting a ball from bin \(B\) given that a black ball was selected from bin \(A\):**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    Bin \(B\) has 3 balls labeled \$1 and 1 ball labeled \$7, so the total number of balls in bin \(B\) is \(3 + 1 = 4\).
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    The probability of selecting a ball from bin \(B\) given that a black ball was selected from bin \(A\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    P(\text{ball from } B \mid \text{black from } A) = \frac{3}{4}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 4. **Calculate the probability of selecting a ball from bin \(W\) given that a white ball was selected from bin \(A\):**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    Bin \(W\) has 5 balls labeled \$8 and 1 ball labeled \$500, so the total number of balls in bin \(W\) is \(5 + 1 = 6\).
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    The probability of selecting a ball from bin \(W\) given that a white ball was selected from bin \(A\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    P(\text{ball from } W \mid \text{white from } A) = \frac{5}{6}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 5. **Calculate the expected value of the amount won:**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    The expected value \(E\) is the sum of the products of the amount won and the probability of each outcome:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    E = P(\text{black from } A) \cdot P(\text{ball from } B \mid \text{black from } A) \cdot \text{amount from } B + P(\text{white from } A) \cdot P(\text{ball from } W \mid \text{white from } A) \cdot \text{amount from } W
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    Substituting the values we have:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    E = \left(\frac{4}{5}\right) \cdot \left(\frac{3}{4}\right) \cdot 1 + \left(\frac{1}{5}\right) \cdot \left(\frac{5}{6}\right) \cdot 7
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    Simplify the expression:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    E = \frac{4 \cdot 3}{5 \cdot 4} + \frac{1 \cdot 5}{5 \cdot 6} \cdot 7 = \frac{3}{5} + \frac{5}{30} \cdot 7 = \frac{3}{5} + \frac{35}{30} = \frac{3}{5} + \frac{7}{6}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    To add these fractions, find a common denominator:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \frac{3}{5} = \frac{18}{30}, \quad \frac{7}{6} = \frac{35}{30}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    E = \frac{18}{30} + \frac{35}{30} = \frac{53}{30}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    Therefore, the expected win is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \boxed{\frac{53}{30}}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]

[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m [prompt] system
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m You are a helpful AI Assistant, designed to provide well-reasoned and detailed responses. You FIRST think about the reasoning process step by step and then provide the user with the answer. Please enclose your final answer in the box: \boxed{Your Answer}.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m user
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m Bin $A$ has one white ball and four black balls.  Bin $B$ has three balls labeled $\$1$ and one ball labeled $\$7$.  Bin $W$ has five balls labeled $\$8$ and one ball labeled $\$500$.  A game is played as follows: a ball is randomly selected from bin $A$.  If it is black, then a ball is randomly selected from bin $B$; otherwise, if the original ball is white, then a ball is randomly selected from bin $W$.  You win the amount printed on the second ball selected.  What is your expected win?
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m assistant
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m [response] To determine the expected win in the game, we need to calculate the expected value of the amount won based on the probability of selecting each type of ball from bins \(A\) and \(B\), and then from bin \(W\).
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 1. **Calculate the probability of selecting a black ball from bin \(A\):**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    Bin \(A\) has 4 black balls and 1 white ball.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    P(\text{black from } A) = \frac{4}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    If a black ball is selected from bin \(A\), a ball is randomly selected from bin \(B\). Bin \(B\) has 3 balls labeled \$1 and 1 ball labeled \$7.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    P(\text{ball from } B \mid \text{black from } A) = \frac{3}{4}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    The expected value of the second ball selected if a black ball is drawn from bin \(A\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    E(\text{second ball} \mid \text{black from } A) = 1 \cdot \frac{3}{4} + 7 \cdot \frac{1}{4} = \frac{3}{4} + \frac{7}{4} = \frac{10}{4} = 2.5
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    Therefore, the total expected value if a black ball is drawn from bin \(A\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    E(\text{win} \mid \text{black from } A) = 2.5 \cdot \frac{4}{5} = 2
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 2. **Calculate the probability of selecting a white ball from bin \(A\):**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    P(\text{white from } A) = \frac{1}{5}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    If a white ball is selected from bin \(A\), a ball is randomly selected from bin \(W\). Bin \(W\) has 5 balls labeled \$8 and 1 ball labeled \$500.
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    P(\text{ball from } W \mid \text{white from } A) = \frac{5}{6}
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    The expected value of the second ball selected if a white ball is drawn from bin \(A\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    E(\text{second ball} \mid \text{white from } A) = 8 \cdot \frac{5}{6} + 500 \cdot \frac{1}{6} = \frac{40}{6} + \frac{500}{6} = \frac{540}{6} = 90
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    Therefore, the total expected value if a white ball is drawn from bin \(A\) is:
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    E(\text{win} \mid \text{white from } A) = 90 \cdot \frac{1}{5} = 18
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 3. **Calculate the total expected value of the win:**
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    E(\text{win}) = P(\text{black from } A) \cdot E(\text{win} \mid \text{black from } A) + P(\text{white from } A) \cdot E(\text{win} \mid \text{white from } A)
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \[
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    E(\text{win}) = \frac{4}{5} \cdot 2 + \frac{1}{5} \cdot 18 = \frac{8}{5} + \frac{18}{5} = \frac{26}{5} = 5.2
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m    \]
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m 
[36m(TaskRunner pid=3930)[0m Therefore, the expected win is \(\boxed{5.2}\).
